  1import chess
  2import pygame

 12class Game:
 13    def __init__(self, screen: pygame.Surface, board: chess.Board, images: dict[str, str]) -> None:
 14        logger.debug("Initializing Game logic")
 15        self.board     = board
 16        self.players   = {"white": Player(chess.WHITE), "black": Player(chess.BLACK)}
 17        self.moves     = dict()
 18        self.last_move = None
 19        self.game_end  = False
 20        self.move_num  = 1
 21        self.images    = images
 22        self.screen    = screen
 23
 24        # Předání zvukového souboru hráčům při jejich inicializaci
 25        self.move_sound = pygame.mixer.Sound(io.BytesIO(base64.b64decode(ASSETS["move-sound"])))
 26        
 27        # Předání zvuku hráčům
 28        self.players["white"].set_move_sound(self.move_sound)
 29        self.players["black"].set_move_sound(self.move_sound)
 30
 31    def loop(self, events: tuple[pygame.event.Event, ...], multiplayer=None) -> None:
 32        if not self.game_end:
 33            if multiplayer == "client":
 34                if self.board.turn == chess.BLACK:
 35                    self.players["black"].on_move(self.board, events)
 36                    self.game_state = "On turn: Black"
 37            elif multiplayer == "server":
 38                if self.board.turn == chess.WHITE:
 39                    self.players["white"].on_move(self.board, events)
 40                    self.game_state = "On turn: White"
 41            else:
 42                if self.board.turn == chess.WHITE:
 43                    self.players["white"].on_move(self.board, events)
 44                    self.game_state = "On turn: White"
 45                else:
 46                    self.players["black"].on_move(self.board, events)
 47                    self.game_state = "On turn: Black"
 48            
 49            draw_board(self.board, self.screen, (self.players["white"], self.players["black"]), self.images)
 50
 51            if self.board.outcome() != None:
 52                self.game_state = f"Game ended: {self.board.outcome().result}"
 53                self.game_end_menu.state = self.game_state
 54                self.game_end = True
 55
 56            self.screen.blit(FONT.render(self.game_state, True, FONT_COLOR), (710,0))
 57            try:
 58                if self.board.peek() != self.last_move:
 59                    self.last_move = self.board.peek()
 60                    self.moves[self.move_num] = self.last_move
 61                    self.move_num += 1
 62            except IndexError:
 63                pass
 64            print_game_log(self.screen, self.moves)
 65
 66
 67class Player:
 68    def __init__(self, color: bool) -> None:
 69        logger.debug("Initializing Player")
 70        self.is_playing      = False
 71        self.color           = color
 72        self.selected_piece  = None
 73        self.selected_square = None
 74        self.move_sound      = None  # Inicializace move_sound jako None
 75        
 76    def set_move_sound(self, move_sound: pygame.mixer.Sound) -> None:
 77        """Přiřadí zvukový efekt pro pohyb do hráče."""
 78        self.move_sound = move_sound
 79
 80    def on_move(self, board: chess.Board, events: tuple[pygame.event.Event, ...]) -> None:
 81        for event in events:
 82            if event.type == pygame.MOUSEBUTTONDOWN:
 83                mouse_pos = pygame.mouse.get_pos()
 84                if mouse_pos[0] >= 50 and mouse_pos[1] >= 50:
 85                    x = int((mouse_pos[0]-50) // SQUARE_SIZE)
 86                    y = 7 - int((mouse_pos[1]-50) // SQUARE_SIZE)
 87                    square = chess.square(x, y)
 88                    piece = board.piece_at(square)
 89
 90                    if self.selected_piece:
 91                        if square == self.selected_square:
 92                            self.selected_piece = None
 93                            self.selected_square = None
 94                            logger.debug(f"Player {get_color(self.color)} cancelled move")
 95                        elif board.color_at(square) == self.color:
 96                            self.selected_piece = piece
 97                            self.selected_square = square
 98                            logger.debug(f"Player {get_color(self.color)} reselected piece {chess.piece_name(self.selected_piece.piece_type)}")
 99                        else:
100                            move = chess.Move(self.selected_square, square)
101                            if move in board.legal_moves:
102                                board.push(move)
103                                logger.debug(f"Player {get_color(self.color)} moved piece {chess.piece_name(self.selected_piece.piece_type)} from {chess.square_name(self.selected_square)} to {chess.square_name(square)}")
104                                
105                                # Přehrát zvuk po provedení tahu
106                                self.play_move_sound()
107                                self.selected_piece = None
108                                self.selected_square = None
109                    elif piece:
110                        if piece.color == self.color:
111                            self.selected_piece = piece
112                            self.selected_square = square
113
114    def play_move_sound(self):
115        """Přehrát zvuk pohybu figurky."""
116        if self.move_sound:  # Ověření, zda je zvuková soubor přiřazen
117            self.move_sound.play()
118

121class AI:
122    def __init__(self, color: bool, difficulty: str) -> None:
123        logger.debug("Initializing AI")
124        self.difficulty     = difficulty
125        self.color          = color
126        self.selected_piece = None  # Přidání atributu selected_piece
127        self.capture_sound = pygame.mixer.Sound(io.BytesIO(base64.b64decode(ASSETS["capture"])))  # Zvuk pro zachycení
128
129    def on_move(self, board: chess.Board, events: tuple[pygame.event.Event, ...]) -> chess.Move:
130        "DO NOT REMOVE EVENTS, Game class will parse events"
131        if self.difficulty == "easy":
132            move = self.easy_move(board)
133        elif self.difficulty == "medium":
134            move = self.medium_move(board)
135        elif self.difficulty == "hard":
136            move = self.hard_move(board)
137        elif self.difficulty == "Fales":
138            move = self.fales_move(board)
139        else:
140            raise ValueError("Difficulty not selected")
141
142        if move:
143            if board.is_capture(move):  # Kontrola, zda tah vede k zachycení figury
144                self.capture_sound.play()  # Přehrání zvuku pro zachycení
145            board.push(move)
146            self.selected_piece = None  # Reset selected_piece po tahu
147            logger.debug("AI moved piece")
148        return move
149
150    def easy_move(self, board: chess.Board) -> chess.Move:
151        """AI s náhodnými tahy, počká 1 vteřinu před výběrem."""
152        time.sleep(1)  # Počkejte 1 sekundu
153        return random.choice(list(board.legal_moves))  # Vybírá náhodný legální tah
154
155    def medium_move(self, board: chess.Board) -> chess.Move:
156        """AI prioritizující zachycení a kontrolu centrálních polí."""
157        legal_moves = list(board.legal_moves)
158        capture_moves = [move for move in legal_moves if board.is_capture(move)]
159        center_squares = [chess.D4, chess.E4, chess.D5, chess.E5]
160
161        # Prioritizace zachycení figury
162        if capture_moves:
163            return random.choice(capture_moves)
164
165        # Prioritizace kontroly centrálních polí
166        central_moves = [move for move in legal_moves if move.to_square in center_squares]
167        if central_moves:
168            return random.choice(central_moves)
169
170        # Pokud není zachycení ani kontrola centra, zvolí náhodný tah
171        return random.choice(legal_moves)
172
173    def hard_move(self, board: chess.Board) -> chess.Move:
174        """AI hledá nejlepší tah s důrazem na agresivitu."""
175        best_move  = None
176        best_value = -9999
177
178        for move in board.legal_moves:
179            board.push(move)
180            board_value = self.evaluate_board(board)
181            board.pop()
182
183            # Zvýšená hodnota pro agresivní tahy (zachycení a kontrola centra)
184            if board.is_capture(move):
185                board_value += 5
186            elif move.to_square in [chess.D4, chess.E4, chess.D5, chess.E5]:
187                board_value += 3
188
189            if board_value > best_value:
190                best_value = board_value
191                best_move = move
192
193        return best_move
194
195    def fales_move(self, board: chess.Board) -> chess.Move:
196        """AI s hlubokou analýzou tahů."""
197        best_move, _ = self.minimax(board, depth=3, maximizing_player=True)
198        return best_move
199
200    def minimax(self, board: chess.Board, depth: int, maximizing_player: bool = True) -> tuple[None, int] | tuple[chess.Move, int]:
201        if depth == 0 or board.is_game_over():
202            return None, self.evaluate_board(board)
203
204        best_move = None
205        if maximizing_player:
206            best_value = -9999
207            for move in board.legal_moves:
208                board.push(move)
209                _, value = self.minimax(board, depth - 1, False)
210                board.pop()
211
212                if value > best_value:
213                    best_value = value
214                    best_move = move
215        else:
216            best_value = 9999
217            for move in board.legal_moves:
218                board.push(move)
219                _, value = self.minimax(board, depth - 1, True)
220                board.pop()
221
222                if value < best_value:
223                    best_value = value
224                    best_move = move
225        return best_move, best_value
226        
227    def evaluate_board(self, board: chess.Board) -> int:
228        """Hodnotí pozici na šachovnici."""
229        if board.is_checkmate():
230            return 10000 if board.turn == chess.BLACK else -10000
231        if board.is_stalemate() or board.is_insufficient_material():
232            return 0
233
234        piece_values = {
235            chess.PAWN: 1,
236            chess.KNIGHT: 3,
237            chess.BISHOP: 3,
238            chess.ROOK: 5,
239            chess.QUEEN: 9,
240            chess.KING: 0
241        }
242
243        value = 0
244        for piece in board.piece_map().values():
245            piece_value = piece_values[piece.piece_type]
246            value += piece_value if piece.color == self.color else -piece_value
247
248        # Přidání strategického hodnocení
249        value += self.position_score(board)
250
251        return value
252
253
254    def position_score(self, board: chess.Board) -> int:
255        """Vyhodnocení pozice na základě umístění figur."""
256        score = 0
257        piece_square_values = {
258            chess.PAWN: [0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0],
259            chess.KNIGHT: [-5, -4, -3, -3, -3, -3, -4, -5],
260            chess.BISHOP: [-4, -2, -1, -1, -1, -1, -2, -4],
261            chess.ROOK: [-2, -1, 0, 0, 0, 0, -1, -2],
262            chess.QUEEN: [-1, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, -1],
263            chess.KING: [0, 1, 1, 3, 3, 1, 1, 0],
264        }
265
266        for square, piece in board.piece_map().items():
267            piece_value = piece_square_values[piece.piece_type]
268            if piece.color == self.color:
269                score += piece_value[square // 8]
270            else:
271                score -= piece_value[square // 8]
272
273        return score
274
275def get_color(color: bool) -> str:
276    return "white" if color==True else "black"
277    
278def init_game(debug=False, name=__name__) -> tuple[pygame.Surface, chess.Board, log.Logger, pygame.time.Clock, Dict[str, pygame.Surface], pygame.font.Font]:
279    global logger
280    os.chdir(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)))
281    logger = log.getLogger(name)
282    if debug:
283        log.basicConfig(level=log.DEBUG, format='%(asctime)s - [%(name)s] - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')
284    else:
285        log.basicConfig(level=log.WARNING,  format='%(asctime)s - [%(name)s] - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')
286    logger.debug("Initializing app")
287
288    logger.debug("Initializing pygame")
289    pygame.init()
290    screen = pygame.display.set_mode((WIDTH, HEIGHT))
291    logger.debug("Initializing chess board logic")
292    board = chess.Board()
293    logger.debug("Initializing frame limiter")
294    clock = pygame.time.Clock()
295
296    logger.debug("Loading images")
297    images = load_images(debug)
298    return screen, board, logger, clock, images
299
300def load_images(debug=False) -> Dict[str, pygame.Surface]:
301    # Určte cestu k kořenovému adresáři projektu (Czess)
302    project_dir = os.path.abspath(os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..", ".."))  # Dva kroky zpět k Czess
303    assets_dir = os.path.join(project_dir, "assets")  # Cesta k assets složce
304
305    images = {}
306    pieces = ["king", "queen", "rook", "bishop", "knight", "pawn", "square"]
307    colors = ["white", "black"]
308
309    if debug:
310        for piece in pieces:
311            for color in colors:
312                img_path = os.path.join(assets_dir, piece, f"{color}.png")
313                try:
314                    img = pygame.image.load(img_path)
315                except FileNotFoundError:
316                    logger.error(f"Image not found: {img_path}")
317                    continue
318                
319                if piece == "square":
320                    img = pygame.transform.scale(img, (SQUARE_SIZE, SQUARE_SIZE))
321                else:
322                    img = pygame.transform.scale(img, (SQUARE_SIZE-(IMAGE_OFFSET*2), SQUARE_SIZE-(IMAGE_OFFSET*2)))
323                
324                images[f"{color}_{piece}"] = img
325                logger.debug(f"Succesfully loaded {color}_{piece} from {img_path}")
326
327        img_path = os.path.join(assets_dir, "ChessBoard.png")
328        try:
329            img = pygame.image.load(img_path)
330            images["chess_board"] = img
331            logger.debug(f"Succesfully loaded chess_board from {img_path}")
332        except FileNotFoundError:
333            logger.error(f"Image not found: {img_path}")
334                    
335        return images
336    else:
337        for piece in pieces:
338            for color in colors:
339                try:
340                    img_b64 = ASSETS[f"{color}_{piece}"]
341                except KeyError:
342                    img_b64 = ERROR_IMAGE
343                    logger.error(f"! Could not load image of {color} {piece}, using error image")
344                
345                img_data = base64.b64decode(img_b64)
346                img_bytes = io.BytesIO(img_data)
347                img = pygame.image.load(img_bytes)
348                
349                if piece == "square":
350                    img = pygame.transform.scale(img, (SQUARE_SIZE, SQUARE_SIZE))
351                else:
352                    img = pygame.transform.scale(img, (SQUARE_SIZE-(IMAGE_OFFSET*2), SQUARE_SIZE-(IMAGE_OFFSET*2)))
353                
354                images[f"{color}_{piece}"] = img
355                if img_b64 == ERROR_IMAGE:
356                    logger.debug("Succesfully loaded error image")
357                else:
358                    logger.debug(f"Succesfully loaded {color}_{piece}")
359        
360        # Načítání chess boardu
361        try:
362            img_b64 = ASSETS[f"chess_board"]
363        except KeyError:
364            img_b64 = ERROR_IMAGE
365            logger.error(f"! Could not load image of chess board, using error image")
366        
367        img_data = base64.b64decode(img_b64)
368        img_bytes = io.BytesIO(img_data)
369        img = pygame.image.load(img_bytes)
370        images[f"chess_board"] = img
371        if img_b64 == ERROR_IMAGE:
372            logger.debug("Succesfully loaded error image")
373        else:
374            logger.debug("Succesfully loaded chess_board")
375        
376        return images
377
378def draw_piece(piece: chess.Piece, screen: pygame.Surface, pos: tuple[int, int], piece_images: Dict[str, pygame.Surface]) -> None:
379    color = get_color(piece.color)
380    type  = chess.piece_name(piece.piece_type)
381    x, y  = pos
382    x     = x*SQUARE_SIZE+IMAGE_OFFSET+50
383    y     = y*SQUARE_SIZE+IMAGE_OFFSET+50
384    img   = piece_images[f"{color}_{type}"]
385
386    screen.blit(img, (x, y))
387
388def draw_square_overlay(screen: pygame.Surface, row: int, col: int) -> None:
389    pygame.draw.rect(screen, (128, 255, 128), (col * SQUARE_SIZE+50, row * SQUARE_SIZE+50, SQUARE_SIZE, SQUARE_SIZE), width=15)
390
391def draw_board(board: chess.Board, screen: pygame.Surface, players: tuple[Player, Player], images: Dict[str, pygame.Surface]) -> None:
392    legal_moves = None
393    screen.fill(EGGSHELL)
394    screen.blit(images["chess_board"], (0, 0))
395
396    if board.turn == chess.WHITE:
397        if players[0].selected_piece:
398            row = 7 - chess.square_rank(players[0].selected_square)
399            col = chess.square_file(players[0].selected_square)
400            pygame.draw.rect(screen, (0, 255, 0), (col * SQUARE_SIZE+50, row * SQUARE_SIZE+50, SQUARE_SIZE, SQUARE_SIZE))
401            legal_moves = [move for move in board.legal_moves if move.from_square == players[0].selected_square]
402    else:
403        if players[1].selected_piece:
404            row = 7 - chess.square_rank(players[1].selected_square)
405            col = chess.square_file(players[1].selected_square)
406            pygame.draw.rect(screen, (0, 255, 0), (col * SQUARE_SIZE+50, row * SQUARE_SIZE+50, SQUARE_SIZE, SQUARE_SIZE))
407            legal_moves = [move for move in board.legal_moves if move.from_square == players[1].selected_square]
408
409    if legal_moves:    
410        for move in legal_moves:
411            row = 7 - chess.square_rank(move.to_square)
412            col = chess.square_file(move.to_square)
413            draw_square_overlay(screen, row, col)
414
415    x = 0
416    y = 0
417    for char in list(board.board_fen()):
418        if char == "/":
419            x = 0
420            y += 1
421        elif char.isnumeric():
422            x += int(char)
423        else:
424            piece = chess.Piece.from_symbol(char)
425            draw_piece(piece, screen, (x, y), images)
426            x += 1
427
428def print_game_log(screen: pygame.Surface, moves: Dict[int, chess.Move]) -> None:
429    if moves:
430        if len(moves) > 15:
431            moves = dict(list(moves.items())[-15:])
432        x = FONT_SIZE + 5
433        n = 1
434        for index, move in moves.items():
435            text = f"{index}. {move.uci()}"
436            screen.blit(FONT.render(text, True, FONT_COLOR), (710,x))
437            x += FONT_SIZE + 5
438            n += 1
439    else:
440        screen.blit(FONT.render("No moves", True, FONT_COLOR), (710,FONT_SIZE+5))
441
442pygame.font.init()
443WIDTH, HEIGHT   = 1200, 700 # 600 x 600 herní pole
444MENU_WIDTH, MENU_HEIGHT = 800, 600
445SQUARE_SIZE     = 600 // 8  # 75
446IMAGE_OFFSET    = 2         # Image size = 71x71
447ROWS, COLS      = 8, 8
448WHITE           = (255, 255, 255)
449FONT_TITLE      = pygame.font.Font(None, 64)
450FONT_OPTION     = pygame.font.Font(None, 50)
451FONT_HELP       = pygame.font.Font(None, 30)
452SHADOW_COLOR    = (128, 119, 97)
453HIGHLIGHT_COLOR = (187, 250, 245)
454FONT_COLOR      = (130, 179, 175)
455BACKGROUND_COLOR= (222, 210, 177)
456EGGSHELL        = (235, 236, 208)
457BLACK           = (0, 0, 0)
458FONT_COLOR      = BLACK
459FONT_SIZE       = 30

class Game: 
13class Game:
14    def __init__(self, screen: pygame.Surface, board: chess.Board, images: dict[str, str]) -> None:
15        logger.debug("Initializing Game logic")
16        self.board     = board
17        self.players   = {"white": Player(chess.WHITE), "black": Player(chess.BLACK)}
18        self.moves     = dict()
19        self.last_move = None
20        self.game_end  = False
21        self.move_num  = 1
22        self.images    = images
23        self.screen    = screen
24
25        # Předání zvukového souboru hráčům při jejich inicializaci
26        self.move_sound = pygame.mixer.Sound(io.BytesIO(base64.b64decode(ASSETS["move-sound"])))
27        
28        # Předání zvuku hráčům
29        self.players["white"].set_move_sound(self.move_sound)
30        self.players["black"].set_move_sound(self.move_sound)
31
32    def loop(self, events: tuple[pygame.event.Event, ...], multiplayer=None) -> None:
33        if not self.game_end:
34            if multiplayer == "client":
35                if self.board.turn == chess.BLACK:
36                    self.players["black"].on_move(self.board, events)
37                    self.game_state = "On turn: Black"
38            elif multiplayer == "server":
39                if self.board.turn == chess.WHITE:
40                    self.players["white"].on_move(self.board, events)
41                    self.game_state = "On turn: White"
42            else:
43                if self.board.turn == chess.WHITE:
44                    self.players["white"].on_move(self.board, events)
45                    self.game_state = "On turn: White"
46                else:
47                    self.players["black"].on_move(self.board, events)
48                    self.game_state = "On turn: Black"
49            
50            draw_board(self.board, self.screen, (self.players["white"], self.players["black"]), self.images)
51
52            if self.board.outcome() != None:
53                self.game_state = f"Game ended: {self.board.outcome().result}"
54                self.game_end_menu.state = self.game_state
55                self.game_end = True
56
57            self.screen.blit(FONT.render(self.game_state, True, FONT_COLOR), (710,0))
58            try:
59                if self.board.peek() != self.last_move:
60                    self.last_move = self.board.peek()
61                    self.moves[self.move_num] = self.last_move
62                    self.move_num += 1
63            except IndexError:
64                pass
65            print_game_log(self.screen, self.moves)

class Player: 
 68class Player:
 69    def __init__(self, color: bool) -> None:
 70        logger.debug("Initializing Player")
 71        self.is_playing      = False
 72        self.color           = color
 73        self.selected_piece  = None
 74        self.selected_square = None
 75        self.move_sound      = None  # Inicializace move_sound jako None
 76        
 77    def set_move_sound(self, move_sound: pygame.mixer.Sound) -> None:
 78        """Přiřadí zvukový efekt pro pohyb do hráče."""
 79        self.move_sound = move_sound
 80
 81    def on_move(self, board: chess.Board, events: tuple[pygame.event.Event, ...]) -> None:
 82        for event in events:
 83            if event.type == pygame.MOUSEBUTTONDOWN:
 84                mouse_pos = pygame.mouse.get_pos()
 85                if mouse_pos[0] >= 50 and mouse_pos[1] >= 50:
 86                    x = int((mouse_pos[0]-50) // SQUARE_SIZE)
 87                    y = 7 - int((mouse_pos[1]-50) // SQUARE_SIZE)
 88                    square = chess.square(x, y)
 89                    piece = board.piece_at(square)
 90
 91                    if self.selected_piece:
 92                        if square == self.selected_square:
 93                            self.selected_piece = None
 94                            self.selected_square = None
 95                            logger.debug(f"Player {get_color(self.color)} cancelled move")
 96                        elif board.color_at(square) == self.color:
 97                            self.selected_piece = piece
 98                            self.selected_square = square
 99                            logger.debug(f"Player {get_color(self.color)} reselected piece {chess.piece_name(self.selected_piece.piece_type)}")
100                        else:
101                            move = chess.Move(self.selected_square, square)
102                            if move in board.legal_moves:
103                                board.push(move)
104                                logger.debug(f"Player {get_color(self.color)} moved piece {chess.piece_name(self.selected_piece.piece_type)} from {chess.square_name(self.selected_square)} to {chess.square_name(square)}")
105                                
106                                # Přehrát zvuk po provedení tahu
107                                self.play_move_sound()
108                                self.selected_piece = None
109                                self.selected_square = None
110                    elif piece:
111                        if piece.color == self.color:
112                            self.selected_piece = piece
113                            self.selected_square = square
114
115    def play_move_sound(self):
116        """Přehrát zvuk pohybu figurky."""
117        if self.move_sound:  # Ověření, zda je zvuková soubor přiřazen
118            self.move_sound.play()

def on_move(self, board: chess.Board, events: tuple[pygame.event.Event, ...]) -> None:

class AI: 
122class AI:
123    def __init__(self, color: bool, difficulty: str) -> None:
124        logger.debug("Initializing AI")
125        self.difficulty     = difficulty
126        self.color          = color
127        self.selected_piece = None  # Přidání atributu selected_piece
128        self.capture_sound = pygame.mixer.Sound(io.BytesIO(base64.b64decode(ASSETS["capture"])))  # Zvuk pro zachycení
129
130    def on_move(self, board: chess.Board, events: tuple[pygame.event.Event, ...]) -> chess.Move:
131        "DO NOT REMOVE EVENTS, Game class will parse events"
132        if self.difficulty == "easy":
133            move = self.easy_move(board)
134        elif self.difficulty == "medium":
135            move = self.medium_move(board)
136        elif self.difficulty == "hard":
137            move = self.hard_move(board)
138        elif self.difficulty == "Fales":
139            move = self.fales_move(board)
140        else:
141            raise ValueError("Difficulty not selected")
142
143        if move:
144            if board.is_capture(move):  # Kontrola, zda tah vede k zachycení figury
145                self.capture_sound.play()  # Přehrání zvuku pro zachycení
146            board.push(move)
147            self.selected_piece = None  # Reset selected_piece po tahu
148            logger.debug("AI moved piece")
149        return move
150
151    def easy_move(self, board: chess.Board) -> chess.Move:
152        """AI s náhodnými tahy, počká 1 vteřinu před výběrem."""
153        time.sleep(1)  # Počkejte 1 sekundu
154        return random.choice(list(board.legal_moves))  # Vybírá náhodný legální tah
155
156    def medium_move(self, board: chess.Board) -> chess.Move:
157        """AI prioritizující zachycení a kontrolu centrálních polí."""
158        legal_moves = list(board.legal_moves)
159        capture_moves = [move for move in legal_moves if board.is_capture(move)]
160        center_squares = [chess.D4, chess.E4, chess.D5, chess.E5]
161
162        # Prioritizace zachycení figury
163        if capture_moves:
164            return random.choice(capture_moves)
165
166        # Prioritizace kontroly centrálních polí
167        central_moves = [move for move in legal_moves if move.to_square in center_squares]
168        if central_moves:
169            return random.choice(central_moves)
170
171        # Pokud není zachycení ani kontrola centra, zvolí náhodný tah
172        return random.choice(legal_moves)
173
174    def hard_move(self, board: chess.Board) -> chess.Move:
175        """AI hledá nejlepší tah s důrazem na agresivitu."""
176        best_move  = None
177        best_value = -9999
178
179        for move in board.legal_moves:
180            board.push(move)
181            board_value = self.evaluate_board(board)
182            board.pop()
183
184            # Zvýšená hodnota pro agresivní tahy (zachycení a kontrola centra)
185            if board.is_capture(move):
186                board_value += 5
187            elif move.to_square in [chess.D4, chess.E4, chess.D5, chess.E5]:
188                board_value += 3
189
190            if board_value > best_value:
191                best_value = board_value
192                best_move = move
193
194        return best_move
195
196    def fales_move(self, board: chess.Board) -> chess.Move:
197        """AI s hlubokou analýzou tahů."""
198        best_move, _ = self.minimax(board, depth=3, maximizing_player=True)
199        return best_move
200
201    def minimax(self, board: chess.Board, depth: int, maximizing_player: bool = True) -> tuple[None, int] | tuple[chess.Move, int]:
202        if depth == 0 or board.is_game_over():
203            return None, self.evaluate_board(board)
204
205        best_move = None
206        if maximizing_player:
207            best_value = -9999
208            for move in board.legal_moves:
209                board.push(move)
210                _, value = self.minimax(board, depth - 1, False)
211                board.pop()
212
213                if value > best_value:
214                    best_value = value
215                    best_move = move
216        else:
217            best_value = 9999
218            for move in board.legal_moves:
219                board.push(move)
220                _, value = self.minimax(board, depth - 1, True)
221                board.pop()
222
223                if value < best_value:
224                    best_value = value
225                    best_move = move
226        return best_move, best_value
227        
228    def evaluate_board(self, board: chess.Board) -> int:
229        """Hodnotí pozici na šachovnici."""
230        if board.is_checkmate():
231            return 10000 if board.turn == chess.BLACK else -10000
232        if board.is_stalemate() or board.is_insufficient_material():
233            return 0
234
235        piece_values = {
236            chess.PAWN: 1,
237            chess.KNIGHT: 3,
238            chess.BISHOP: 3,
239            chess.ROOK: 5,
240            chess.QUEEN: 9,
241            chess.KING: 0
242        }
243
244        value = 0
245        for piece in board.piece_map().values():
246            piece_value = piece_values[piece.piece_type]
247            value += piece_value if piece.color == self.color else -piece_value
248
249        # Přidání strategického hodnocení
250        value += self.position_score(board)
251
252        return value
253
254
255    def position_score(self, board: chess.Board) -> int:
256        """Vyhodnocení pozice na základě umístění figur."""
257        score = 0
258        piece_square_values = {
259            chess.PAWN: [0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0],
260            chess.KNIGHT: [-5, -4, -3, -3, -3, -3, -4, -5],
261            chess.BISHOP: [-4, -2, -1, -1, -1, -1, -2, -4],
262            chess.ROOK: [-2, -1, 0, 0, 0, 0, -1, -2],
263            chess.QUEEN: [-1, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, -1],
264            chess.KING: [0, 1, 1, 3, 3, 1, 1, 0],
265        }
266
267        for square, piece in board.piece_map().items():
268            piece_value = piece_square_values[piece.piece_type]
269            if piece.color == self.color:
270                score += piece_value[square // 8]
271            else:
272                score -= piece_value[square // 8]
273
274        return score
AI(color: bool, difficulty: str) 
123    def __init__(self, color: bool, difficulty: str) -> None:
124        logger.debug("Initializing AI")
125        self.difficulty     = difficulty
126        self.color          = color
127        self.selected_piece = None  # Přidání atributu selected_piece
128        self.capture_sound = pygame.mixer.Sound(io.BytesIO(base64.b64decode(ASSETS["capture"])))  # Zvuk pro zachycení
difficulty
color
selected_piece
capture_sound
def on_move( self, board: chess.Board, events: tuple[pygame.event.Event, ...]) -> chess.Move: 
130    def on_move(self, board: chess.Board, events: tuple[pygame.event.Event, ...]) -> chess.Move:
131        "DO NOT REMOVE EVENTS, Game class will parse events"
132        if self.difficulty == "easy":
133            move = self.easy_move(board)
134        elif self.difficulty == "medium":
135            move = self.medium_move(board)
136        elif self.difficulty == "hard":
137            move = self.hard_move(board)
138        elif self.difficulty == "Fales":
139            move = self.fales_move(board)
140        else:
141            raise ValueError("Difficulty not selected")
142
143        if move:
144            if board.is_capture(move):  # Kontrola, zda tah vede k zachycení figury
145                self.capture_sound.play()  # Přehrání zvuku pro zachycení
146            board.push(move)
147            self.selected_piece = None  # Reset selected_piece po tahu
148            logger.debug("AI moved piece")
149        return move

DO NOT REMOVE EVENTS, Game class will parse events

def easy_move(self, board: chess.Board) -> chess.Move: 
151    def easy_move(self, board: chess.Board) -> chess.Move:
152        """AI s náhodnými tahy, počká 1 vteřinu před výběrem."""
153        time.sleep(1)  # Počkejte 1 sekundu
154        return random.choice(list(board.legal_moves))  # Vybírá náhodný legální tah

AI s náhodnými tahy, počká 1 vteřinu před výběrem.

def medium_move(self, board: chess.Board) -> chess.Move: 
156    def medium_move(self, board: chess.Board) -> chess.Move:
157        """AI prioritizující zachycení a kontrolu centrálních polí."""
158        legal_moves = list(board.legal_moves)
159        capture_moves = [move for move in legal_moves if board.is_capture(move)]
160        center_squares = [chess.D4, chess.E4, chess.D5, chess.E5]
161
162        # Prioritizace zachycení figury
163        if capture_moves:
164            return random.choice(capture_moves)
165
166        # Prioritizace kontroly centrálních polí
167        central_moves = [move for move in legal_moves if move.to_square in center_squares]
168        if central_moves:
169            return random.choice(central_moves)
170
171        # Pokud není zachycení ani kontrola centra, zvolí náhodný tah
172        return random.choice(legal_moves)

AI prioritizující zachycení a kontrolu centrálních polí.

def hard_move(self, board: chess.Board) -> chess.Move: 
174    def hard_move(self, board: chess.Board) -> chess.Move:
175        """AI hledá nejlepší tah s důrazem na agresivitu."""
176        best_move  = None
177        best_value = -9999
178
179        for move in board.legal_moves:
180            board.push(move)
181            board_value = self.evaluate_board(board)
182            board.pop()
183
184            # Zvýšená hodnota pro agresivní tahy (zachycení a kontrola centra)
185            if board.is_capture(move):
186                board_value += 5
187            elif move.to_square in [chess.D4, chess.E4, chess.D5, chess.E5]:
188                board_value += 3
189
190            if board_value > best_value:
191                best_value = board_value
192                best_move = move
193
194        return best_move

AI hledá nejlepší tah s důrazem na agresivitu.

def fales_move(self, board: chess.Board) -> chess.Move: 
196    def fales_move(self, board: chess.Board) -> chess.Move:
197        """AI s hlubokou analýzou tahů."""
198        best_move, _ = self.minimax(board, depth=3, maximizing_player=True)
199        return best_move

AI s hlubokou analýzou tahů.

def minimax( self, board: chess.Board, depth: int, maximizing_player: bool = True) -> tuple[None, int] | tuple[chess.Move, int]: 
201    def minimax(self, board: chess.Board, depth: int, maximizing_player: bool = True) -> tuple[None, int] | tuple[chess.Move, int]:
202        if depth == 0 or board.is_game_over():
203            return None, self.evaluate_board(board)
204
205        best_move = None
206        if maximizing_player:
207            best_value = -9999
208            for move in board.legal_moves:
209                board.push(move)
210                _, value = self.minimax(board, depth - 1, False)
211                board.pop()
212
213                if value > best_value:
214                    best_value = value
215                    best_move = move
216        else:
217            best_value = 9999
218            for move in board.legal_moves:
219                board.push(move)
220                _, value = self.minimax(board, depth - 1, True)
221                board.pop()
222
223                if value < best_value:
224                    best_value = value
225                    best_move = move
226        return best_move, best_value

def init_game( debug=False, name='common') -> tuple[pygame.surface.Surface, chess.Board, logging.Logger, pygame.time.Clock, typing.Dict[str, pygame.surface.Surface], pygame.font.Font]: 
279def init_game(debug=False, name=__name__) -> tuple[pygame.Surface, chess.Board, log.Logger, pygame.time.Clock, Dict[str, pygame.Surface], pygame.font.Font]:
280    global logger
281    os.chdir(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)))
282    logger = log.getLogger(name)
283    if debug:
284        log.basicConfig(level=log.DEBUG, format='%(asctime)s - [%(name)s] - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')
285    else:
286        log.basicConfig(level=log.WARNING,  format='%(asctime)s - [%(name)s] - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')
287    logger.debug("Initializing app")
288
289    logger.debug("Initializing pygame")
290    pygame.init()
291    screen = pygame.display.set_mode((WIDTH, HEIGHT))
292    logger.debug("Initializing chess board logic")
293    board = chess.Board()
294    logger.debug("Initializing frame limiter")
295    clock = pygame.time.Clock()
296
297    logger.debug("Loading images")
298    images = load_images(debug)
299    return screen, board, logger, clock, images
def load_images(debug=False) -> Dict[str, pygame.surface.Surface]: 
301def load_images(debug=False) -> Dict[str, pygame.Surface]:
302    # Určte cestu k kořenovému adresáři projektu (Czess)
303    project_dir = os.path.abspath(os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..", ".."))  # Dva kroky zpět k Czess
304    assets_dir = os.path.join(project_dir, "assets")  # Cesta k assets složce
305
306    images = {}
307    pieces = ["king", "queen", "rook", "bishop", "knight", "pawn", "square"]
308    colors = ["white", "black"]
309
310    if debug:
311        for piece in pieces:
312            for color in colors:
313                img_path = os.path.join(assets_dir, piece, f"{color}.png")
314                try:
315                    img = pygame.image.load(img_path)
316                except FileNotFoundError:
317                    logger.error(f"Image not found: {img_path}")
318                    continue
319                
320                if piece == "square":
321                    img = pygame.transform.scale(img, (SQUARE_SIZE, SQUARE_SIZE))
322                else:
323                    img = pygame.transform.scale(img, (SQUARE_SIZE-(IMAGE_OFFSET*2), SQUARE_SIZE-(IMAGE_OFFSET*2)))
324                
325                images[f"{color}_{piece}"] = img
326                logger.debug(f"Succesfully loaded {color}_{piece} from {img_path}")
327
328        img_path = os.path.join(assets_dir, "ChessBoard.png")
329        try:
330            img = pygame.image.load(img_path)
331            images["chess_board"] = img
332            logger.debug(f"Succesfully loaded chess_board from {img_path}")
333        except FileNotFoundError:
334            logger.error(f"Image not found: {img_path}")
335                    
336        return images
337    else:
338        for piece in pieces:
339            for color in colors:
340                try:
341                    img_b64 = ASSETS[f"{color}_{piece}"]
342                except KeyError:
343                    img_b64 = ERROR_IMAGE
344                    logger.error(f"! Could not load image of {color} {piece}, using error image")
345                
346                img_data = base64.b64decode(img_b64)
347                img_bytes = io.BytesIO(img_data)
348                img = pygame.image.load(img_bytes)
349                
350                if piece == "square":
351                    img = pygame.transform.scale(img, (SQUARE_SIZE, SQUARE_SIZE))
352                else:
353                    img = pygame.transform.scale(img, (SQUARE_SIZE-(IMAGE_OFFSET*2), SQUARE_SIZE-(IMAGE_OFFSET*2)))
354                
355                images[f"{color}_{piece}"] = img
356                if img_b64 == ERROR_IMAGE:
357                    logger.debug("Succesfully loaded error image")
358                else:
359                    logger.debug(f"Succesfully loaded {color}_{piece}")
360        
361        # Načítání chess boardu
362        try:
363            img_b64 = ASSETS[f"chess_board"]
364        except KeyError:
365            img_b64 = ERROR_IMAGE
366            logger.error(f"! Could not load image of chess board, using error image")
367        
368        img_data = base64.b64decode(img_b64)
369        img_bytes = io.BytesIO(img_data)
370        img = pygame.image.load(img_bytes)
371        images[f"chess_board"] = img
372        if img_b64 == ERROR_IMAGE:
373            logger.debug("Succesfully loaded error image")
374        else:
375            logger.debug("Succesfully loaded chess_board")
376        
377        return images

379def draw_piece(piece: chess.Piece, screen: pygame.Surface, pos: tuple[int, int], piece_images: Dict[str, pygame.Surface]) -> None:
380    color = get_color(piece.color)

384    y     = y*SQUARE_SIZE+IMAGE_OFFSET+50
385    img   = piece_images[f"{color}_{type}"]

def draw_square_overlay(screen: pygame.surface.Surface, row: int, col: int) -> None: 
389def draw_square_overlay(screen: pygame.Surface, row: int, col: int) -> None:
390    pygame.draw.rect(screen, (128, 255, 128), (col * SQUARE_SIZE+50, row * SQUARE_SIZE+50, SQUARE_SIZE, SQUARE_SIZE), width=15)
def draw_board( board: chess.Board, screen: pygame.surface.Surface, players: tuple[Player, Player], images: Dict[str, pygame.surface.Surface]) -> None: 
392def draw_board(board: chess.Board, screen: pygame.Surface, players: tuple[Player, Player], images: Dict[str, pygame.Surface]) -> None:
393    legal_moves = None
394    screen.fill(EGGSHELL)
395    screen.blit(images["chess_board"], (0, 0))
396
397    if board.turn == chess.WHITE:
398        if players[0].selected_piece:
399            row = 7 - chess.square_rank(players[0].selected_square)
400            col = chess.square_file(players[0].selected_square)
401            pygame.draw.rect(screen, (0, 255, 0), (col * SQUARE_SIZE+50, row * SQUARE_SIZE+50, SQUARE_SIZE, SQUARE_SIZE))
402            legal_moves = [move for move in board.legal_moves if move.from_square == players[0].selected_square]
403    else:
404        if players[1].selected_piece:
405            row = 7 - chess.square_rank(players[1].selected_square)
406            col = chess.square_file(players[1].selected_square)
407            pygame.draw.rect(screen, (0, 255, 0), (col * SQUARE_SIZE+50, row * SQUARE_SIZE+50, SQUARE_SIZE, SQUARE_SIZE))
408            legal_moves = [move for move in board.legal_moves if move.from_square == players[1].selected_square]
409
410    if legal_moves:    
411        for move in legal_moves:
412            row = 7 - chess.square_rank(move.to_square)
413            col = chess.square_file(move.to_square)
414            draw_square_overlay(screen, row, col)
415
416    x = 0
417    y = 0
418    for char in list(board.board_fen()):
419        if char == "/":
420            x = 0
421            y += 1
422        elif char.isnumeric():
423            x += int(char)
424        else:
425            piece = chess.Piece.from_symbol(char)
426            draw_piece(piece, screen, (x, y), images)
427            x += 1
def print_game_log(screen: pygame.surface.Surface, moves: Dict[int, chess.Move]) -> None: 
429def print_game_log(screen: pygame.Surface, moves: Dict[int, chess.Move]) -> None:
430    if moves:
431        if len(moves) > 15:
432            moves = dict(list(moves.items())[-15:])
433        x = FONT_SIZE + 5
434        n = 1
435        for index, move in moves.items():
436            text = f"{index}. {move.uci()}"
437            screen.blit(FONT.render(text, True, FONT_COLOR), (710,x))
438            x += FONT_SIZE + 5
439            n += 1
440    else:
441        screen.blit(FONT.render("No moves", True, FONT_COLOR), (710,FONT_SIZE+5))
